***каспийский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каспийский.html>каспи́йский</a> (21522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Caspius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Caspian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́йский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каспийский.html>каспи́йский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaspíjskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Caspian
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каспийский.html>каспи́йское</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kaspíjskoje</b> móre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Caspian Sea</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***касса.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:касса.html>касса</a> (4473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:касса.html>ка́сса</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kássa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:касса.html>ка́ссы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:касса.html>ка́ссы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:касса.html>ка́сс</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pay desk, cash desk, checkout</li>
<li>ticket window, box office</li>
<li>cash</li>
<li>bank, fund</li>
<li>cash register</li>
<li><i>(polygraphy)</i> case</li></ol>

***кассационный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кассационный.html>кассацио́нный</a> (32024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kassation</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">касса́ция</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kassácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кассационный.html>кассацио́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kassaciónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> appeal, cassation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кассационный.html>кассацио́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалоба.html>жа́лоба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kassaciónnaja</b> žáloba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">appeal</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***кассовый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кассовый.html>ка́ссовый</a> (20942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:касса.html>ка́сса</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kássa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кассовый.html>ка́ссовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kássovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cash desk, cash register
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кассовый.html>ка́ссовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чека.html>чек</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kássovyj</b> ček</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>cash register</b> receipt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cash
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кассовый.html>ка́ссовая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:операция.html>опера́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kássovaja</b> operácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>cash</b> transaction</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> box office
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кассовый.html>ка́ссовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:провал.html>прова́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kássovyj</b> provál</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/box_office_bomb" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:box office bomb"><b>box office</b> bomb</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>successful in box-office terms</li></ol>

***кастрировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кастрировать.html>кастри́ровать</a> (25913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кастрировать.html>кастри́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kastrírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to castrate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">remove the testicles of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кастрюля.html>кастрю́ля</a> (4545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kastrol</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kasserolle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">casserole</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кастрюля.html>кастрю́ля</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kastrjúlja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кастрюля.html>кастрю́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кастрюля.html>кастрю́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кастрюля.html>кастрю́ль</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катастрофа.html>катастро́фа</a> (3608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катастрофа.html>катастро́фа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katastrófa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катастрофа.html>катастро́фы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катастрофа.html>катастро́фы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катастрофа.html>катастро́ф</a></b>)

***катать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a> (11268)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покатать.html>поката́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive (a trolley), to take (somebody) for a drive</li>
<li>to ride (on a bicycle, on a swing, etc.)</li>
<li>to roll <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to cause to revolve</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is in the class of Russian abstract verbs. Its counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>/<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">катну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покатить.html>покати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are concrete verbs.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for derived verbs.</i></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a> (4640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покататься.html>поката́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ride <i>in a vehicle</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>лю́бишь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> са́ночки <a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ljúbišʹ <b>katátʹsja</b>, ljubí i sánočki vozítʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">after the feast comes the reckoning</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">if you like to ride, you should like to pull the sleigh</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to roll <i>(abstract verb), see</i> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>кати́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыр</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сле</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak syr v másle <b>katátʹsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to live in clover</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">to roll like cheese in butter</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́ху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>katátʹsja</b> so sméxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to split one's sides with laughter, to roar with laughter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ride <i>on skis, skates, bicycle, or snowboard</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Katátʹsja</b> na lýžax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ski</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***катафалк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лк</a> (28340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">catafalque</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">catafalco</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*catafalicum</i>, probably derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κατά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fala</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scaffolding, wooden siege tower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katafálk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>catafalque, catafalco</li>
<li>hearse, bier</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:категорически.html>категори́чески</a> (4977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:категорически.html>категори́чески</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kategoríčeski</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>categorically</li>
<li>flatly, strongly, out of hand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:категорически.html>категори́чески</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:возражать.html>возража́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kategoríčeski</b> vozražátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">strongly object</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:категорически.html>категори́чески</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвергать.html>отверга́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kategoríčeski</b> otvergátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reject vigorously</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***катер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>ка́тер</a> (4726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cutter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>ка́тер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">káter</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>ка́тера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>катера́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>катеро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> motorboat, boat <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">with an inboard engine</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cutter</li></ol>
